  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3a564056-41df-41b2-9429-2b5b18453c9c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText4999255741340250006" style="display:none">In the last year, Allie's survived three arrests, two breakups and one family breakdown. The only bright point has been her new life at Cimmeria Academy. It's the one place she's felt she belongs. And the fact that it's brought dark-eyed Carter West into her life hasn't hurt either. But far from being a safe haven, the cloistered walls of Cimmeria are proving more dangerous than Allie could have imagined. The students and faculty are under threat, and Allie's family - from her mysterious grandmother to her runaway brother - are at the centre of the storm. Allie is going to have to choose between protecting her family and trusting her friends. But secrets have a way of ripping even the strongest relationships apart...</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer528875778" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14297074017133952372">4.5 stars ... And wow!<br/>It’s no secret that I didn’t much care for Night School. While I thought there was nothing wrong with it technically, it just didn’t leave much of an impression. But I’ve been known to change my mind before, and I’ve changed my mind this time. Everything C.J. Daugherty failed to do with Night School, she did with Legacy, and then some. The characters were more memorable, the plot was absolutely thrilling, and even the love triangle wasn’t as obnoxious as last time. Quite th</span>
  <span id="freeText14297074017133952372" style="display:none">4.5 stars ... And wow!<br>It’s no secret that I didn’t much care for Night School. While I thought there was nothing wrong with it technically, it just didn’t leave much of an impression. But I’ve been known to change my mind before, and I’ve changed my mind this time. Everything C.J. Daugherty failed to do with Night School, she did with Legacy, and then some. The characters were more memorable, the plot was absolutely thrilling, and even the love triangle wasn’t as obnoxious as last time. Quite the contrary, in fact.<br><br>Before all else, I feel the need to say more about this formerly obnoxious love triangle. I have never in my entire life switched teams mid series, not once, but I suppose there’s a first time for everything. Daugherty expertly manipulated me into liking Carter a lot less, and liking Sylvain infinitely more, and yet I never felt manipulated at all. Other authors <i>have</i> tried, I assure you, it just never worked before. So mark this day on your calendars because I’m about to write something I doubt I’ve ever written before: this love triangle works! Every time Allie changed her mind, I changed mine too, and every time she was confused, I was right there alongside her. I obviously have a favorite now, but she’s already pushed me into changing my mind once, she could just as easily do it again. Brava, Ms. Daugherty. Well done.<br><br>Daugherty showed her ability to successfully transform her characters through more than just Sylvain. Jo was a different person altogether – wounded, insecure and vulnerable after everything she’s been through, but more composed and reliable as well. Some new characters were introduced, and I found them all very interesting, especially Rachel’s father Raj Patel and Sylvain’s friend Nicole. Old enemies were still there, but as soon as the truth about Allie’s family came to light, some new ones showed up as well. <br><br>Just the other day I was sitting here, chatting with a friend and shamelessly making fun of boarding school books (with a few exceptions, of course), and now I am forced to eat my words. Or just add Night School to that very short list of exceptions. I adore Cimmeria Academy. I adore the idea behind it, I adore the teachers and I desperately want to be an advanced Night School student. (Only I’m not very athletic so that would never, ever work.) This series is a new favorite of mine and my expectations for the third book are sky high. <br><br>Legacy doesn’t end with a cliffhanger, but it does have an open ending, so be prepared for quite a few unanswered questions. It didn’t bother me. To be honest, I barely noticed, I was too busy crying and worrying and crying some more. <br><br>Finally, I’m not usually overdramatic, but please allow me to say this: Oh my God, my heart is broken, I doubt I’ll ever, ever (ever!) recover! Please write faster, C.J. Daugherty! <br><br> <a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14297074017133952372" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16531027336581911039">OK, so before I go on my praise fest I just have to say that this was really a slow-starter for me.... I think it was pretty much my fualt, becuase I had to mentally rewind and remember the last book. But, once I got my head in the game, it was on like Donkey Kong! I fell back in love with Allie, Rachel and (especially) Sylvain. Carter drove me insane and I will just say I was happy when the inevitable happened!<br/><br/>If I wasn't clear enough up there, I am 100% team Sylvain... but I typically pick the</span>
  <span id="freeText16531027336581911039" style="display:none">OK, so before I go on my praise fest I just have to say that this was really a slow-starter for me.... I think it was pretty much my fualt, becuase I had to mentally rewind and remember the last book. But, once I got my head in the game, it was on like Donkey Kong! I fell back in love with Allie, Rachel and (especially) Sylvain. Carter drove me insane and I will just say I was happy when the inevitable happened!<br /><br />If I wasn't clear enough up there, I am 100% team Sylvain... but I typically pick the wrong guy, so there's that little problem. Carter was very protective and mistrusting of Allie this time, they just didn't spark for me in this book. All the chemistry seemed to ooze off of Allie-vain ;)<br /><br />And, I have to note how sorry I felt for our girl with her whole brother situation. But, she gave me some proud reader moments. Allie does make bad desicions, but it seems like her heart is always in the right place.<br /><br />I'll say it again, I thought I was over the whole boarding school thing, but these books are so awesome the setting really just adds to the fun!<br /><br />4 stars and my curiosity is on overdrive! C'mon #3!!!!<br /><br /><br /><br />Thankies to my dear friend Tina for sharing! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16531027336581911039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6698137002309203902"><blockquote>

</blockquote><br/>Everything changes for Allie.<br/>She enters the Night School. She finds new friends and loses old. She finds out that the Cimmeria Academy has more secrets than it seems and that Nathaniel has his people everywhere. <br/>In the Night School Allie has to learn to understand when people lie and how they do it, but she does not quite like it because knowing that her closest friends lie to her is painful. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416395ra/822259.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So does Sylvain.   <span id="freeText6698137002309203902" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Le cœur a ses raisons que la raison ne connaît point."</b>
</blockquote><br>Everything changes for Allie.<br>She enters the Night School. She finds new friends and loses old. She finds out that the Cimmeria Academy has more secrets than it seems and that Nathaniel has his people everywhere. <br>In the Night School Allie has to learn to understand when people lie and how they do it, but she does not quite like it because knowing that her closest friends lie to her is painful. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416395ra/822259.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So does Sylvain. So does Carter. And even Allie. <br>Lies are everywhere. People are more and more suspicious of each other. <br>Allie finally realizes that Carter is not the person he pretends to be. She understands, that everything is more complicated and that Carter takes her freedom. While Allie is just confused and scared about her feelings and sometimes a bit too suspicious Carter is different. <br>He is possessive, sometimes he even seems obsessed with Allie. He does not believe in her and it hurts. She needs faith and she understands, that Carter cannot give her faith. <br>She also realizes that Sylvain changed. He is a better person in this book. Caring, soft and thoughtful. He helps Allie more than once, he risks everything for her. And what is far more important- He believes in her. <br>Now lies are not the only problem anymore. The main problem, like in the first book, is trust. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416395i/822260.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Whom can Allie trust? Can she trust Sylvain? Should she trust him? And what about Carter? And Rachel with whom Allie grows apart? <br>What about Jo, who acts more and more suspicious and whose personality is not steady any more?<br><br>Gabe reappears and he is black-hearted. Moreover, Allie's lost brother contacts her again and his letter tears Allie apart.<br>Allie has not enough information. Neither about Nathaniel, nor about the Night School and her grandmother Lucinda. But Allie knows that she needs this information. <br>She simply has to understand what it really going on and what the conflict is truly about...<br><br>This book is absolutely breathtaking, it is filled with danger and fear and suspicion. The dark and tensed atmosphere captures from the first until the very last page. <br>The tension in this book is nearly tangible! I like the first book, but I really love the second one! <br>The love-triangle finally moves to the background so it does not disturb the plot and its progression. I love the love triangle in this book, especially because it is completely comprehensible. <br>I love all the character and I love the fact that the book animates to ask questions and be suspicious!! <br><br>I highly recommend this book to everyone! It is an enjoyable read that make you look forward to the third book! :) </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13810271153281562423">Just as amazing as book 1, if not better!<br/><br/>Legacy begins following the aftermath of Night School, with Allie on the run from people trying to hurt her. She immediately returns to Cimmeria, but because of everything that has already happened, she, quite rightly, is confused on who she can trust, and who is out to hurt her.   <span id="freeText13810271153281562423" style="display:none">Just as amazing as book 1, if not better!<br /><br />Legacy begins following the aftermath of Night School, with Allie on the run from people trying to hurt her. She immediately returns to Cimmeria, but because of everything that has already happened, she, quite rightly, is confused on who she can trust, and who is out to hurt her. The events of Legacy ramp up the action we already saw in Night School, making the series much more enjoyable and full of suspense.<br /><br />Allie really starts to come into her own in this book, starting to deal with what Night School expects from her, whilst all the while trying to work out who to trust. All of the characters evolved in this book, some for the better, some for the worse, which is a credit to Daugherty to make me like characters I really hadn't earlier, and vice versa, especially Sylvain.<br /><br />A lot of information comes out in this book, especially to do with Allie and her heritage, and yet again, the events at the end of the novel made me raring to read more.<br /><br />I would definitely recommend this amazing UKYA Book to everyone!</span>

<div id="review_381639669" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/381639669" />
    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381639669?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=own-copy">own-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=mystery-thriller">mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=whodunit">whodunit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381639669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17835920239337800823">4.5 stars<br/><br/>I quickly fell in love with C.J Daugherty debut novel, Night School. It has everything I adore in an escape; mystery, action, romance and thrilling characters. It also has this brilliant quality of being crazy consuming! I couldn't wait to see what Daugherty had in store for these characters next and I'm happy to say that Legacy turned out to be another favorite.<br/><br/><b>Legacy</b> starts off with Allie on the run from men in suits who are chasing her through the London streets. Soon she finds refug</span>
  <span id="freeText17835920239337800823" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />I quickly fell in love with C.J Daugherty debut novel, Night School. It has everything I adore in an escape; mystery, action, romance and thrilling characters. It also has this brilliant quality of being crazy consuming! I couldn't wait to see what Daugherty had in store for these characters next and I'm happy to say that Legacy turned out to be another favorite.<br /><br /><b>Legacy</b> starts off with Allie on the run from men in suits who are chasing her through the London streets. Soon she finds refuge with Rachel's family and are back in Cimmeria Academy before term begins. The attack at the school left the academy in devastation and everyone works hard to rebuild the old gothic building before all the students come back. It's here that Isabelle tells Allie that she will be admitted into Night School, where she will learn how to protect herself from Nathaniel's men.<br />Only, Night School is a lot harder then Allie realized, physically, emotionally and morally. <br />Rules and secrets have a way of trapping you but lies and betrayal have a mind of it's own and soon Allie will have to decide where her true loyalties belong, no matter who she may lose in the process.<br /><br />First off, I want to take a minute and just gush about the excellent writing style! I'm not sure what it is about Daugherty's books that have this all absorbing quality to it, but if I would have to pick one word to describe it, I guess it would be realistic. These characters and everything that happens in this book just feels so dame real! Vividly detailed, Daugherty has an exquisite flavor when she writes. From lavish details about the school and it's grounds, to every expression on each of these faces, to the fight scenes and clever witty dialog and banter. Every little aspect is set to motion where I feel like I'm transported in these pages and I can see everything in all it's richness. Then we have this incredibly maddening mysterious plot, and when I say mysterious, I mean I'm still not exactly sure what Night School is all about. <br />When you read a vampire book, you expect vampires to be in it. Same with werewolves, fairies and so on. But the beauty of this book is that it's like a label-less can. Daugherty doesn't give you all the answers, even in the second book, we're still not positively positive what's inside. This is both alluring as hell and aggravating, but funny enough it's not frustrating. In fact, I love not knowing, it only makes me want to read these books more!<br /><br />I simply adore ever single one of these characters, even the bad dudes. They're all skillfully well developed. Allie felt so conflicted this year, with all that's happening at the academy plus all the vigorous training in Night School, not to mention her very daunting love life and all the family drama. Poor girl has had one helluva year. But Allie is such a resilient character. Solid and strong, she doesn't let things weigh her down long. She takes responsibility for things that she did wrong, learns from her mistakes and changes and grows because of them. She is definitely a character I can be proud of.<br />There really isn't any secondary characters in this book, or at least not for me. Everyone seems to have a very specific role and are quite involved with every aspect of the story, which I find fascinating and fun.<br />Jo, Rachel, Jules, Isabella, Lucas, Carter and Sylvain continue to bring in much entertainment as the story slowly starts to unfold. We even have a couple of new characters, Zoe Glass, our kickass zingy child-genius that is infectiously adorable and Nicole, who turned out to be a pleasant surprise.<br />There is a spy among us within the walls of Cimmeria Academy. It was fun to try to guess whodunit, but sadly, it will keep you guessing and leave you hanging till the next installment.<br /><br />As for Allie's love life? Well, I wish I could be happy about that particular part of the story, but I'd be lying if I said I was. I'm the kind of reader who doesn't mind love triangles, but this one stabbed me in the heart. In all honestly, I don't think I would have minded so much if Carter stayed true to his character. In the first book, Carter West was hard to read and I couldn't quite get a fix on him, but he was still sweet, charming and a supportive friend and love interest. So it really shocked the hell out of me (and broke my heart) to see this overbearing, possessive, difficult and unreasonable Carter that unfortunately graced us in this book. He's still Carter, but he's...different, wrong somehow and I just didn't like it.<br />I'm all for giving second chances to characters who prove redeemable, and Sylvain has proven time and time again that he regrets what he did, but I'm not happy with this new romantic development. Sure, he may have been the better man this round, but I don't feel any chemistry when Allie and Sylvain are together. He had his chance in the first book and blew it. End of story, but hey, they can still be friends. <br />So yes, I'm waving my 'Team Carter' flag proudly in hopes that he doesn't let me down and things play out differently in later books. <br /><br />Bottom line, I seriously couldn't love a series more. It's crazy addicting, outstanding writing and real heart and soul characters that have you invested at minute one. This is without a doubt one of the most intense and intriguing stories I ever read. It's grips you and doesn't let go till the very last page and even then it will consume your thoughts long after the story is done. The ending shattered my heart and there is still so much we don't know and so much we still need to learn, so I can't begin to express how badly I need the next book!<br />A must read for fans who enjoy mystery-suspense, thrilling action and an unstoppable romance. <br /><br />MORE!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="17835920239337800823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_398540014" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/398540014" />
    <a title="Sandra " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9752625-sandra"><img alt="Sandra " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345749155p2/9752625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/398540014?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra " href="/user/show/9752625-sandra">Sandra </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=panic-attack">panic-attack</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=reviewed-books">reviewed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=awesome-characters">awesome-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sexy-males">sexy-males</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer398540014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8062652736121166260">I will start my review by saying - AMAZING! This book is so amazing. I'm sure the third one in the series will be just as good. I just hope we don't have to wait too long.<br/><br/>I couldn't get into it in the beginning because it's been a year since i'v read the first one <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12576579.Night_School__Night_School___1_' title='Night School (Night School, #1) by C.J. Daugherty' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352303569s/12576579.jpg' alt='Night School (Night School, #1) by C.J. Daugherty' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a>, and i found it sometimes hard to remember who is who. But as i read throughout the book, i started to recognized those who i forgotten. Thank god for that! It was much more less confusing.<br/><br/>I'v waited so long for book 2 to come out</span>
  <span id="freeText8062652736121166260" style="display:none">I will start my review by saying - AMAZING! This book is so amazing. I'm sure the third one in the series will be just as good. I just hope we don't have to wait too long.<br><br>I couldn't get into it in the beginning because it's been a year since i'v read the first one <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12576579.Night_School__Night_School___1_" title="Night School (Night School, #1) by C.J. Daugherty" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352303569s/12576579.jpg" alt="Night School (Night School, #1) by C.J. Daugherty" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, and i found it sometimes hard to remember who is who. But as i read throughout the book, i started to recognized those who i forgotten. Thank god for that! It was much more less confusing.<br><br>I'v waited so long for book 2 to come out, and when i found it in my mail, i nearly fainted. You have no idea how much i craved this book after the 1st one. I actually COULDN'T SLEEP AT NIGHT! I'm not joking.<br><br>I love everything about this book, this series, this author, every bloody thing! And to be honest, i did have some issues with it, but now i have totally forgotten what they were. All i can see is this marvelous book.<br><br>I was so happy to be able to connect with the characters once again. I LOVE them ALL. Especially the main protagonist, Allie. Allie and her friends were all kick-ass and awesome, some had some serious issues and were very sarcastic. But that's what i like! I felt like i was there with Allie, feeling her emotions and seeing things through her eyes, that was wayyyy cool. <br><br>****<br>"' I don't want...' He pulled her tightly against him - so close that she could feel the heat radiating from his body. ' I don't want to hurt you'. A frown flitted across her face. ' You wouldn't ever do that.'<br>****<br> <br>DO NOT read the 2sc book before reading the 1st. Oh yh, and for those who don't know, there IS a love triangle. <br><br>****<br>' with her right hand still resting against his chest, she lifted his hand with her left and placed it against her heart so he could feel it pounding.<br>" See?" She said. " We both feel the same thing." His eyes darkening, he kissed her so hard she fell backwards, and they both tumbled to the polished wood floor.'<br>****<br><br>Overall, even though it wasn't as good as book 1, it was damn well close, and i still loved it so much! I knew i wouldn't be disappointed. Night School Legacy had everything i was looking for - action, romance, drama, and even a touch of mystery and thriller. YOU HAVE TO READ THIS!!! <br><br>That's it for the non spoiler section. If you want to read this series or just check it out, then please don't hesitate because it's totally worth it, trust me. So, if you have read this book, or the 1st, and you don't mind to be spoiled then stay and read on! We'll be discussing some things. <br><br>I wasn't sure about Allie joining the Night School thiny, i don't know why, but it felt like she was walking into something bad, and i hated all the 'mystery' and secrets about it. It just gave me the creeps. But as she started to train and stuff, i actually extremely liked it. I only wish that the author would have introduce/described more about the training, like she did on Allie's first day. We knew exactly what she was being taught and what she was doing. I found it all very fascinating and intriguing. <br><br>And there we have the love triangle between Allie, Carter and Sylvain. If you would ask me which team am i on before i read the second book, i wouldn't have hesitated and immediately say " Carter all the way", but now? I'm no longer so sure. Although, i think i'm leaning a tiny, tiny, tiny bit more towards Carter, still. <br><br><br><br>~SPOILER ALERT~<br>The only reason why i'm leaning more towards Carter is because Sylvain tried to rape Allie in book 1. I'm very curious as to WHY he would try such a thing, since it seemed like he cared about her. I would actually really appreciate it if Miss/Mrs Daughtery would explain that in maybe book 3 or something.<br>***************<br><br>*****Discussion/spoiler.***** <br>Let's talk about the Allie and Nicolie kissing. When Nicolie came up to Allie and juts kissed her, i was bloody hell MORTIFIED and embarrassed for her so much i literally wanted to crawl underneath the ground, and stay there. WHY!? WHY did she kiss her? I don't understand, i really don't get that. And when Allie didn't do anything and just stood there, i was like " What the hell is going on with her? Is she like turning into a lesbian or something?" If i was in her place i would be swearing and pushing the girl as far away from me as possible. That was a bit unrealistic. <br>****************************<br><br>The ending was like " OMG! OMG! NO!" for me. I was at the edge of my seat, constantly gasping for breath. It can't end like this! What the hell?! Are you like serious? AHHH, the torture awaits me. God knows how long i'll have to wait for book 3 to come out! They should have some mercy here. Like, some people NEED peaceful sleep once in a while. I don't know how i can handle it without reading the next book immediately. God help me!<br><br>*****SPOILER!*****<br>I don't like it how we don't know if she's going to stay with Sylvain or get back with Crater. Dammit! I'm changing my mind here! I want her to end up with Carter. They belong together, Sylvain can end up with that Nicolie girl or someone else. I'm back on team Carter! I love him! And i DO NOT like it how they broken up, at all. Makes me wanna punch Carter for not fighting for her and trying to sort things out together. <br>*******************<br><br>Can't wait to read book 3. How about you? what did you think?<br><br></span>

<div id="review_512504001" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/512504001" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4011534-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299995914p2/4011534.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/512504001?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/4011534-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4011534-lisa?shelf=hachette">hachette</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer512504001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5657270958631249972">Originally posted at <a href='http://www.readmebookmarkmeloveme.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read Me Bookmark Me Love Me</a><br/><br/>Night School was easily one of my favourite reads of 2012, and although Legacy isn't quite as good, I still found myself loving it. Daugherty's writing is addictive as always, and you'll pass a large handful of hours reading this without even realising it. Upon starting, I immediately connected with the characters I loved so much again and it was like the year-long wait never existed. <br/><br/>When Allie Sheridan went back to London for the holidays, she di</span>
  <span id="freeText5657270958631249972" style="display:none">Originally posted at <a href="http://www.readmebookmarkmeloveme.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read Me Bookmark Me Love Me</a><br /><br />Night School was easily one of my favourite reads of 2012, and although Legacy isn't quite as good, I still found myself loving it. Daugherty's writing is addictive as always, and you'll pass a large handful of hours reading this without even realising it. Upon starting, I immediately connected with the characters I loved so much again and it was like the year-long wait never existed. <br /><br />When Allie Sheridan went back to London for the holidays, she didn't expect to be chased down by a group of Nathaniel's agents, or to be returning to Cimmeria Academy early to help repair fire damages caused by her brother, Christopher. At first, things seem to be going well. Allie and Carter are super adorable and sexy, and there's some funny awkward tiptoeing around Sylvain, since he saved her life post-rape attempt. Unfortunately, our smiles don't last for long as things quickly spiral out of control. The secrets, misunderstandings and total lack of communication are monumental in Legacy. As much as I love Allie and Carter, I don't know whether to bury my head in the sand in defeat or to run away screaming.<br /><br />In this sequel, the plot thickens as Nathaniel's motives are explained, and as he takes bigger risks in order to get what he desires, the students at Cimmeria are put in unpredictable danger. As a result, Allie is admitted into Night School where the focus is now on self defence and they soon learn that there's a traitor amongst them. One of the members of Night School or staff is Nathaniel's inside spy and so the Night School students are forced to interview another member assigned to them in search of any inconsistencies, with lying leading to expulsion. It sounds simple enough....BUT OF COURSE NOT, THIS IS FICTION!<br /><br />This leads us to the dirty, frustrating mess that is Allie and Carter's relationship. Not too far into Legacy, Carter transforms into an overprotective, controlling jerk who completely forbids Allie from seeing Sylvain. They can't be friends or even acquaintances. With Sylvain's past behaviour, I understand his concern but this was too much and clearly NOT just about her safety at all. Carter, come here so I can slap the stupid out of you! Unfortunately for us and Allie, everything snowballs from there. Allie's put in difficult situations with horrible timing, and absolutely nothing works out for her, with Carter or her non-Night School friends! My heart was an ugly little mess by the end of this novel. I feel so much for her, even though at times I felt she needed to be slapped too. Everything that happened with Allie was either wrong or unfair and it was horrible! #AngstWimp<br /><br />As a character, I really did like Allie (for the most part). She does well in Night School, albeit with a shaky start, and tries her best to solve all of the mysteries around her while dodging Gabe who seems to be popping up everywhere. The small clues combined with the subtle foreshadowing and my halfway-there theories have me curious and desperately awaiting the next book. Legacy seems to pose more questions than answers, and I was a little let down that the plot development wasn't huge. I was hoping for a bit more to happen, for a few more answers to come our way, but sadly it looks like that'll have to wait for book three.<br /><br />Despite all of the heartache Daugherty made me feel, she still managed to keep me laughing with her well-placed moments of wit and humour, and her captivating story will keep you wanting to know what will happen next. Legacy gives us more insight into some of the characters, especially Carter, while making us distrust others. This novel feels somewhat unresolved because of the sheer amount of unanswered questions, but filled with intrigue and dangerous charm, Legacy is an entertaining sequel which will hopefully pave the way to an explosive third book. I have no idea how things will end and I'm honestly a little afraid after these latest developments! </span>
  <a data-text-id="5657270958631249972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_474364287" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/474364287" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474364287?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=for-review-read">for-review-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=british-author">british-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474364287" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18439515007842559180">I really enjoyed Night School so I was excited to get my hands on a copy of the sequel Legacy and couldn't wait to see what would happen next in the story. After the revelations made at the end of the first book I was really interested to see how things would play out for Allie now she had learnt some of her family secrets. She certainly had an unusual introduction to life at Cimmeria Academy over the summer and the start of the new year looked set to be just as explosive. I can't fault the open</span>
  <span id="freeText18439515007842559180" style="display:none">I really enjoyed Night School so I was excited to get my hands on a copy of the sequel Legacy and couldn't wait to see what would happen next in the story. After the revelations made at the end of the first book I was really interested to see how things would play out for Allie now she had learnt some of her family secrets. She certainly had an unusual introduction to life at Cimmeria Academy over the summer and the start of the new year looked set to be just as explosive. I can't fault the opening to Legacy, action packed and fast paced I was on the edge of my seat desperate to see how Allie would get out of the situation she had found herself in. Unfortunately once she arrived at the Academy I felt that the plot really slowed down and I ended up disappointed.<br /><br />One of the things I loved most about Night School was how action packed it was but Legacy felt much more character driven. That isn't necessarily a bad thing but I like some kind of plot to go along with the character development. In this case very little actually seemed to happen, everyone continued to keep Allie in the dark, she got practically no more information about her family or what was actually going on and why Nathaniel was so determined to plot against the school. By the end of the book I don't feel I have answers to any of my questions and I was left feeling frustrated. I was also shocked at the behaviour of some of the characters, it seemed like Carter and Sylvain had completely switched personalities from the first book. I loved Carter before but in this instalment he was a complete idiot and the way he treated Allie made me so angry I wanted to punch something. On the other hand Sylvain, whose actions in the first book are still completely unforgivable, has turned into a really nice guy. I was shocked to find myself liking Sylvain and I did actually start to believe that he was sorry for the things he did before but in my mind that doesn't make them any more excusable and I still have a hard time letting that go.<br /><br />Unfortunately Legacy definitely suffered with second book syndrome for me, I hate to give negative reviews but I was so bored that I almost stopped reading. The book is nearly 400 pages long and practically nothing happens, the only thing that kept me going to the end was my love for the first book. The main element of the book is relationship angst between Allie, Carter and Sylvain which is something I just wasn't interested in reading about. If it hadn't had such a major focus it wouldn't have bothered me but I found it all too much. After the action packed beginning you really have to wait until the last 20 pages for anything to happen and then I felt things were rushed over too quickly and we missed out on a lot of potential excitement.<br /><br />I don't want to put people off reading the story because I definitely seem to be in the minority with this one - a lot of other bloggers have been giving it very high ratings. I have to be honest with my reviews though and tell you how I really feel about the books I read or there is no point in me even writing reviews in the first place. I'm sure I will pick up the next book in the series, I have so many unanswered questions about everything and I do really like Allie and want to know what happens to her. I just hope that I enjoy the next book as much as I enjoyed Night School.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18439515007842559180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16605238945455077869">3.5 stars<br/><br/>Oh my brain hurts! This second installment of the Night School series was beyond entertaining, but has left me with so many unanswered questions! My head is spinning from everything we did learn and begging for more answers.<br/><br/>Legacy starts off with Allie being chased and let me tell you my heart was pounding! She of course gets away and for her safety she goes to live with her friend Rachel until school starts. When it does start things don't get any easier for Allie. She is behind her Ni</span>
  <span id="freeText16605238945455077869" style="display:none">3.5 stars<br /><br />Oh my brain hurts! This second installment of the Night School series was beyond entertaining, but has left me with so many unanswered questions! My head is spinning from everything we did learn and begging for more answers.<br /><br />Legacy starts off with Allie being chased and let me tell you my heart was pounding! She of course gets away and for her safety she goes to live with her friend Rachel until school starts. When it does start things don't get any easier for Allie. She is behind her Night School training, her friends aren't happy about this new addition to her schedule, there is a spy among her peers that she can't find, and Carter *sigh* I don't even know where to being with him. My heart is broken =(<br /><br />This book isn't big on answers, but it is filled with action and while I love action I still need answers. I feel like this book took a small step back and I am a little disappointed. I had so many questions from the last book that I couldn't wait to have answered and the author doesn't even really touch on any of them. Even her characters were getting fed up with the lack of information given. So since this book wasn't filled with answers you want to know what to expect?? HEARTACHE! Lots and lots of heartache. I understand that Allie needed to breathe and I seriously wanted to kick Carter for his ultimatum, but these needed to TALK! I can't believe the way their story ended in this one and I just don't know what to do. I was always a Team Carter so Allies new relationship is not sitting well with me and I just hope the author rights this wrong early on in the next book and gives us some answers! One of the things I liked about the first book was the secrets and smoke and mirror stuff, but I can only take so much of that before I start losing interest. <br /><br />There is one thing that happens that I can't actually talk about, but I am very upset about it and very confused. I hope we also get closure in regards to this situation that happens at the end. I want this something to have more meaning for the person involved.<br /><br />Even though I have a headache and heartache I still did enjoy this installment. Allie is feisty as ever and I still enjoyed reading her story. I will say though that if the next book doesn't start explaining things I might have a different opinion</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1970561301537722615">I’m pissed. <br/><br/>I really hoped I’ll like this series. However, from the beginning I didn’t care much for what’s going on, and as I read more pages I got frustrated and then the book suddenly ended and I was pissed. What a stupid ending! At the end of the first book we were left with a bunch of questions and I think it wouldn’t be too much to think they would be answered in this book, at least some of them. Of course, that’s not what happens. We get a few bread crumbs of answers with MORE questions. </span>
  <span id="freeText1970561301537722615" style="display:none">I’m pissed. <br /><br />I really hoped I’ll like this series. However, from the beginning I didn’t care much for what’s going on, and as I read more pages I got frustrated and then the book suddenly ended and I was pissed. What a stupid ending! At the end of the first book we were left with a bunch of questions and I think it wouldn’t be too much to think they would be answered in this book, at least some of them. Of course, that’s not what happens. We get a few bread crumbs of answers with MORE questions. I guess now we know why there are five books in the series.<br /><br />And the characters… is it me or did they all of sudden become idiots?<br /><br />Another thing that annoyed me was the love triangle. I thought that ended in the first book, but apparently not… apparently Allie is in love with Sylvain now…</span>
  <a data-text-id="1970561301537722615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11808330327997951736">This series definitely is going downhill. The first book was brilliant and deserved the 5-star rating, as for this one, it was nothing more than Allie puzzling over her relationship as a riddle. There was nothing going on throughout the first half of the book and then at the end we're thrown a mind-blowing plot twist. <br/>Allie is able to fight like a tiger after two or three self-defence lessons. She can do almost everything but, surprisingly, can't focus when she's on duty. The only thing she thin</span>
  <span id="freeText11808330327997951736" style="display:none">This series definitely is going downhill. The first book was brilliant and deserved the 5-star rating, as for this one, it was nothing more than Allie puzzling over her relationship as a riddle. There was nothing going on throughout the first half of the book and then at the end we're thrown a mind-blowing plot twist. <br />Allie is able to fight like a tiger after two or three self-defence lessons. She can do almost everything but, surprisingly, can't focus when she's on duty. The only thing she thinks about is her personal life, namely - to kiss or not to kiss. <br />Personaly, I fancy those two boys; however, I do believe the story itself shouldn't revolve around them.<br /><br />The plot. <br /><br />What do we have here? Allie is back at school and she helps the staff renovate the building before the school starts. Then about 200 pages we're presented with Allie learning how to fight and figuring out whom she fancies. Then a traitor shows up and I feel like this intrigue will continue till the last book comes out. She also finds out about her relative and who she's connected with. That's basically it. <br /><br />This series is over for me. Officially. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11808330327997951736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3281866558" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3281866558" />
    <a title="Paula  Phillips" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1969584-paula-phillips"><img alt="Paula  Phillips" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574564336p2/1969584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3281866558?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula  Phillips" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula  Phillips" href="/user/show/1969584-paula-phillips">Paula  Phillips</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3281866558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16403211808143785890">Recently, I was talking about my Top Ten Tuesday of books I have had on my Kindle for ages and keep meaning to read and so today with that post on my mind I decided to read Legacy - Book #2 of the Night School Series. In Legacy, Allie had returned home for the break after the incident where her brother Christopher burned down the school and then their friend Gabe killed one of their other friends Ruth. Just before Allie is due back to school, she is almost accosted by four guys in suits. Seeing </span>
  <span id="freeText16403211808143785890" style="display:none">Recently, I was talking about my Top Ten Tuesday of books I have had on my Kindle for ages and keep meaning to read and so today with that post on my mind I decided to read Legacy - Book #2 of the Night School Series. In Legacy, Allie had returned home for the break after the incident where her brother Christopher burned down the school and then their friend Gabe killed one of their other friends Ruth. Just before Allie is due back to school, she is almost accosted by four guys in suits. Seeing the guys she remembers Isabelle's - the headmistress's warning and runs. She then is saved by Mr. Patel who is Rachel's dad and spends her remaining break time with Rachel's family. The girls along with their closest friends return to the school before school starts to help fix some of the damage caused by the fire. During this time, Isabelle gives Allie some news about her family and the truth of who her Grandmother is - this surprises Allie as she never realized that her mother came from wealth and that her Grandmother is one of the most powerful women of the world. We later find out that the reason Allie was targeted is because of her grandmother as a way to smoke her out. Nathaniel wants the power from Lucille Meldrum- Allie's Grandmother. Legacy is an action-packed novel whereas you read it will be difficult for Allie to figure out who to trust and who is betraying the school as there is an inside mole for Nathaniel. I have to admit some of the characters in this book I liked e.g Zoe Glass was one of my favorites and others like Carter - freaking annoyed me as seriously you do not own Allie and can't dictate her life, family and friendships. Anyway, if you love UK Boarding School novels and Adventure/Spy stories then check out The Night School series by C.J Daugherty today.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16403211808143785890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_486372788" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/486372788" />
    <a title="Celine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6180856-celine"><img alt="Celine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362210418p2/6180856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/486372788?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celine" href="/user/show/6180856-celine">Celine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6180856-celine?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6180856-celine?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6180856-celine?shelf=atom-hachette">atom-hachette</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer486372788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5807519579055418878">Review originally posted in: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/2013/04/195-book-review-legacy.html'>http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/...</a><br/><br/><u>Cover:</u><br/>Love the snowy theme of the cover and also the building that represents the academy! The red colour of Allie's hair and the font are also a good contrast to the white background.<br/><br/><u>Story:</u><br/><br/><b>Something dark is threatening Cimmeria Academy...</b><br/><br/>A year ago, I read Night School and absolutely loved it! The dark story about murders in an academy full of secrets was such an intriguing and exciting read I couldn't put the book down at all</span>
  <span id="freeText5807519579055418878" style="display:none">Review originally posted in: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/2013/04/195-book-review-legacy.html">http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/...</a><br /><br /><u>Cover:</u><br />Love the snowy theme of the cover and also the building that represents the academy! The red colour of Allie's hair and the font are also a good contrast to the white background.<br /><br /><u>Story:</u><br /><br /><b>Something dark is threatening Cimmeria Academy...</b><br /><br />A year ago, I read Night School and absolutely loved it! The dark story about murders in an academy full of secrets was such an intriguing and exciting read I couldn't put the book down at all. When I heard that there was a sequel, I was ecstatic and after finishing Legacy, I believe that the sequel is even better than the first book!<br /><br />In Legacy, Allie returns back to the academy and continues her life as a student. She is also in a relationship with the 'dreamy' Carter West. Everything sounds perfect, right? But the secrets surrounding Allie and the academy are still a threat and also endanger the students of the academy. The most interesting thing about this book is unravelling all these secrets and mysteries. I love how C.J. Daugherty brought us into some sort of treasure hunt to find all the clues to unlock the secrets and mysteries of the academy and by the end of the book, everything will finally make sense. The murders, the deaths, the betrayals, the romance, they are all pieces of puzzles that when finally assembled, create the 'bigger' picture. The romance in this book, shifts from Allie and Carter to Allie and Sylvain too. This shift is also a part of the secrets and mysteries. The ending left me breathless and I can't wait for the third book in the series!<br /><br /><u>Characters:</u><br />I still adored Allie in this book even though some of her actions and behaviours annoyed me. She is trying to adapt in the academy after all the murders and events in the first book, also trying to have a normal relationship with Carter but alas, the secrets and mysteries cannot stay hidden and become a threat to Allie. This in return, also strains her relationship with Carter who has his own secrets and makes Allie switch to Sylvain for protection, care and someone she can trust with no secrets. I loved Carter and disliked Sylvain in the first book but somehow, C.J. Daugherty manages to switch the situation around and I ended up hating Carter and starting to like Sylvain throughout Legacy. Carter becomes too over-protective of Allie which I hated because he was over-protective but never explained to Allie what was happening in the academy. Sylvain, on the other hand, started off as a friend to Allie (after their relationship was damaged in the first book) but their relationship became more. Sylvain became someone who Allie can rely on, someone she can trust, someone who would listen to her and support her decisions. I enjoyed reading about the other characters from the first book in Legacy but Allie, Carter and Sylvain are definitely the characters that stood out the most for me!<br /><br /><u>Overall:</u><br />Legacy is the amazing sequel to Night School, bringing you a story full of secrets, mysteries with a perfect amount of romance! C.J. Daugherty's writing will take you on a journey to unlock all these secrets, mysteries and the end will leave you breathless. Absolutely can't wait for the third book!<br /><br /><b>Thank you Hachette Australia for the review copy!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5807519579055418878" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer491224926740483378"><b> Actual rating 4.5 </b><br/>Ahhhhh maaaaaaaaaaaaan!!!<br/>So I literally just finished it and I feel like I want to do all sorts of things right now. <br/>First of all a happy dance (many of them involved with this book - first I did one when my bookstore told me my copy had arrived, then when things got exciting, and now after having finished it and thinking that this series is amazing).<br/>Second, I am at loss of words due to the thing with Jo at the end. <br/>No spoilers, so I won't say what happened but if you've read </span>
  <span id="freeText491224926740483378" style="display:none"><b> Actual rating 4.5 </b><br />Ahhhhh maaaaaaaaaaaaan!!!<br />So I literally just finished it and I feel like I want to do all sorts of things right now. <br />First of all a happy dance (many of them involved with this book - first I did one when my bookstore told me my copy had arrived, then when things got exciting, and now after having finished it and thinking that this series is amazing).<br />Second, I am at loss of words due to the thing with Jo at the end. <br />No spoilers, so I won't say what happened but if you've read it - CRAZY HUH?? :(<br />Third, I am sad I can't bring myself to give this book full 5 stars. <br />It's just that this was my most anticipated release of 2013 and I had very high hopes that were not quite met in the beginning half of the book, not at all. <br />I was so disappointed to tell you the truth. <br />Well thank you to C.J. Daugherty for coming up with amazing twists around halfway through that had me glued to the pages again the same way book one had!<br /><br />Another weird thing happened:<br />I'm starting to like Sylvain. <br />HOW IS THAT EVEN POSSIBLE AFTER BOOK ONE??<br />Well I don't know but I really understand Allie's feelings towards him and he seems rather genuine in this book. <br />Yep - I even like him despite his accent.<br />I know that many girls start drooling when boys have foreign accents but to me, especially when I read about it in books, it sounds rather cringey and not desirable at all usually haha. <br />So yeah Sylvain, congratulations!<br /><br />And Carter *.*<br />At first I was bored with their relationship in this book as it's not particularly investing to read about a happy clappy relationship. <br />However, things start happening that change everything and now I don't know what (or who) I want for Allie.<br />Okay secretly I do somehow <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ CARTER  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Haha.<br />If you loved Night School as much as I did and can endure a slow start that absolutely kicks off though, I'd very very highly recommend Night School Legacy to you!</span>

She's happy with Carter, finally knows about her family and why she's at her place in Cimmeria.   <span id="freeText3525893223520701467" style="display:none">Allie entered the Night School and she seems very happy to have extra work. She's happy with Carter, finally knows about her family and why she's at her place in Cimmeria. Still, I'm not sure really much happens because it is kind of messy. There is still little action, and despite everything being dangerous, they all act like nothing is happening. It is pretty stupid to see, and I really wonder why I bother reading this story because it makes no sense.<br /><br />The love triangle is still not resolved and it is getting stupid. But then I guess it was stupid from the start.<br />I still dislike Carter, but I'm no team Sylvain. Allie still acts like a little kid and is still a moron but she is growing up and I'm starting to actually like her.<br />And I'm glad to see friendship taking a good part of the story and Zoe is the best addition to the cast.<br /><br />And once again, the author ended the book with a grand final. <span id="freeTextContainer6348942386479064724">Oh no!!!I don't like the end!!! I just can't belive it. I cried with this book three times:<br/>1. when Carter and Allie broke up- i wasn't happy<br/>2. when Sylvain and Allie got back together- i wasn't happy<br/>3. when my second favorite character(Carter will always be the first) died- i wasn't happy<br/>Ok, so now five things i think about Allie after second book:<br/>1. she is still stupid<br/>2. it's her folt for-i don't know-EVERYTHING!!!<br/>3. she didn't trust Carter- so she is an idiot<br/>4. she trusted Sylvain- so she is a</span>
  <span id="freeText6348942386479064724" style="display:none">Oh no!!!I don't like the end!!! I just can't belive it.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer387922191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9721387135127644457"><b>
  <b> ***CONTAINS MASSIVE SPOILER*** also a massive spoiler from Amanda Hocking's Switched series </b>
</b><br/><br/><br/>Just like the first book, this one is amazing. Seriously my favourite series in a while! This reminds me of the love triangle in the Switched series by Amanda Hocking. Wendy ended up with Loki when I first started they books I wanted her to be with Finn but then in the last book I wanted Loki and that's who she ends up with too... And in this book I wanted her to end up with Sylvain and not Carter (l</span>
  <span id="freeText9721387135127644457" style="display:none"><b>
  <b> ***CONTAINS MASSIVE SPOILER*** also a massive spoiler from Amanda Hocking's Switched series </b>
</b><br /><br /><br />Just like the first book, this one is amazing. Seriously my favourite series in a while! This reminds me of the love triangle in the Switched series by Amanda Hocking. Wendy ended up with Loki when I first started they books I wanted her to be with Finn but then in the last book I wanted Loki and that's who she ends up with too... And in this book I wanted her to end up with Sylvain and not Carter (like I did in the first book, wanted her to be with Carter) I'm not sure who she will end up with though I'm hoping for Sylvain and for Carter to end up with Jules. I absolutely love Nicole! I wish she was in it more, hopefully the next book. I can't believe Jo died, it was so unfair, she was an amazing character!! I also love Zoe more than anything, she's so strange and weird and I love it! This book was very unpredictable although I predicted that Nathaniel was going to be like Isabelle's brother or something, step-brother is close enough though, right? I can't believe I finished this book so fast, it felt like I had just started reading it and then it was finished! That's when you know you've got a good book in your hands!! Rachel is great too and I'm happy she's with Lucas! I really cannot wait for the next book, like this one I will be getting it as soon as it's out! I can't wait to see what happens :) </span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('t4lkwLPzc2IBJ+6kVMwVxo5zn48EG42p5laDmcFcJB4tBbmvWoTidRLPHsgDjoYzJNkwtnhIvjVzNP8oqtsdTA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ONG7G9XCiP+tMWmRqnufj+2f0UkI2VEjgrF0UOsCHeCiXWZ0PLUZ6L7Zmf39OQx6RzV+cHSKYr8X0wjhgIUksg==')})
  }
//]]>

            if ($('bookCover_17978510').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_17978510').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
